Symbolic Identifiers

  • ## (value; Lib, mlibUseful)
  • && (value; bossLib, simpLib)
  • * (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • + (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)

  • - (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • -- (value; Parse)
  • --> (value; FinalType)
  • / (value; Arbrat)
  • ::> (value; mlibSubst)
  • < (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • <= (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • == (value; Parse, mlibUseful)
  • > (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • >* (value; Coding)
  • >- (value; Coding, errormonad, lcsymtacs, optmonad, seqmonad, smpp, stmonad)
  • >-> (value; Coding, optmonad, seqmonad)
  • >= (value; Arbintcore, Arbnumcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibArbnum, mlibOmegaint)
  • >> (value; Coding, errormonad, lcsymtacs, mlibParser, optmonad, seqmonad, smpp, stmonad)
  • >>++ (value; mlibParser)
  • >| (value; lcsymtacs)
  • ?> (value; Lib)
  • @> (value; mlibSubst)
  • |-> (constructor; mlibUseful)
  • |-> (value; Lib)
  • |<>| (value; mlibSubst)
  • |> (value; Lib, liteLib)
  • || (value; Coding, mlibParser, smpp)
  • ||| (value; smpp)
  • ~ (value; Arbintcore, Arbrat, mlibArbint, mlibOmegaint)
